The communication server is based upon a well-known CouchDB database system and can be integrated with existing database setups, such as SAP, and can be configured separately to include services and to manage user accounts. The internal communication framework of Vizario allows for connectivity to different server-side services, such as MQTT Brokers for live-data visualization and import into Desktop and Hololens devices.\r\n\r\nVizario is not designed to produce fancy marketing-style visualizations in the first place. It was built by a group of AR experts with a combined 50+ years experience in Augmented Reality technology, with more than 2 years constant feedback from workers on the shopfloor. The driving force behind the concept of the Vizario framework is productivity and ease-of-use for non-AR experts.
